under construction:Undocumented Class

The ADComputePlaneSmallStrain has not been documented. The content listed below should be used as a starting point for documenting the class, which includes the typical automatic documentation associated with a MooseObject; however, what is contained is ultimately determined by what is necessary to make the documentation clear for users.


# ADComputePlaneSmallStrain

!syntax description /Materials/ADComputePlaneSmallStrain

## Overview

!! Replace these lines with information regarding the ADComputePlaneSmallStrain object.

## Example Input File Syntax

!! Describe and include an example of how to use the ADComputePlaneSmallStrain object.

!syntax parameters /Materials/ADComputePlaneSmallStrain

!syntax inputs /Materials/ADComputePlaneSmallStrain

!syntax children /Materials/ADComputePlaneSmallStrain

Compute a small strain under plane stress assumption

Input Parameters

  • displacementsThe displacements appropriate for the simulation geometry and coordinate system

    C++ Type:std::vector

    Options:

    Description:The displacements appropriate for the simulation geometry and coordinate system

Required Parameters

  • base_nameOptional parameter that allows the user to define multiple mechanics material systems on the same block, i.e. for multiple phases

    C++ Type:std::string

    Options:

    Description:Optional parameter that allows the user to define multiple mechanics material systems on the same block, i.e. for multiple phases

  • blockThe list of block ids (SubdomainID) that this object will be applied

    C++ Type:std::vector

    Options:

    Description:The list of block ids (SubdomainID) that this object will be applied

  • boundaryThe list of boundary IDs from the mesh where this boundary condition applies

    C++ Type:std::vector

    Options:

    Description:The list of boundary IDs from the mesh where this boundary condition applies

  • computeTrueWhen false, MOOSE will not call compute methods on this material. The user must call computeProperties() after retrieving the MaterialBase via MaterialBasePropertyInterface::getMaterialBase(). Non-computed MaterialBases are not sorted for dependencies.

    Default:True

    C++ Type:bool

    Options:

    Description:When false, MOOSE will not call compute methods on this material. The user must call computeProperties() after retrieving the MaterialBase via MaterialBasePropertyInterface::getMaterialBase(). Non-computed MaterialBases are not sorted for dependencies.

  • constant_onNONEWhen ELEMENT, MOOSE will only call computeQpProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps.When SUBDOMAIN, MOOSE will only call computeSubdomainProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps. Evaluations on element qps will be skipped

    Default:NONE

    C++ Type:MooseEnum

    Options:NONE ELEMENT SUBDOMAIN

    Description:When ELEMENT, MOOSE will only call computeQpProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps.When SUBDOMAIN, MOOSE will only call computeSubdomainProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps. Evaluations on element qps will be skipped

  • eigenstrain_namesList of eigenstrains to be applied in this strain calculation

    C++ Type:std::vector

    Options:

    Description:List of eigenstrains to be applied in this strain calculation

  • global_strainOptional material property holding a global strain tensor applied to the mesh as a whole

    C++ Type:MaterialPropertyName

    Options:

    Description:Optional material property holding a global strain tensor applied to the mesh as a whole

  • out_of_plane_directionzThe direction of the out-of-plane strain.

    Default:z

    C++ Type:MooseEnum

    Options:x y z

    Description:The direction of the out-of-plane strain.

  • out_of_plane_strainNonlinear variable for plane stress condition

    C++ Type:std::vector

    Options:

    Description:Nonlinear variable for plane stress condition

  • volumetric_locking_correctionFalseFlag to correct volumetric locking

    Default:False

    C++ Type:bool

    Options:

    Description:Flag to correct volumetric locking

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_sqexp_cartesian_10_10_rho_0_sample_9.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_sqexp_cartesian_10_10_rho_0_sample_9.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D/sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_6/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    d = d

    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'

  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  [../]

    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D_qualitative/gold/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = %s
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = %s
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [../]

    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain

    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'

  [../]

  [../]

  [../]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors

    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [../]
[]

[Materials]

    initial_stress = 't 0 0 0 t 0 0 0 0'
    eigenstrain_name = 'is'

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]

    out_of_plane_strain = 'strain_zz'
    eigenstrain_names = 'is'
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'

  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = 'd'
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]

    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate critical_fracture_energy'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = 'd'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = 'd'
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = FixedPointTransient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels -snes_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200        200                0                     vinewtonrsls'
  dt = 1e-3
  end_time = 0.22

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-12
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-08

  fp_max_its = 10
  fp_tol = 1e-03

  automatic_scaling = true
  compute_scaling_once = false
[]

[Outputs]
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    file_base = 'visualize'
    hide = 'bounds_dummy'
  [../]
  [./console]
    type = Console
    outlier_variable_norms = false
  [../]
[]
Close

    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = '0.5 Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    coefficient = 0.1

      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]

      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]

  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D_qualitative/sqexp_cartesian_5_25_rho_0_seed_g/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_sqexp_cartesian_5_25_rho_0_seed_g.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_sqexp_cartesian_5_25_rho_0_seed_g.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'

  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true

  print_linear_residuals = false

    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]

  [../]

    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_5_5_rho_0_sample_4.txt
  [../]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]

examples/mud_2D/sqexp_cartesian_5_5_rho_0.5_sample_10/mechanical.i

  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]

  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

  [../]
  [./disp_y]

  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'

  [../]

  [../]

    coefficient = 0.1

      variable = disp_x

      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]

    type = DirichletBC

    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]

    value = 0

    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false

examples/mud_2D/exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_3/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_3.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_3.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [../]

    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'

    variable = strain_zz

      secondary = 'right'

      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]

      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]

      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]

    type = DirichletBC

    [../]

    [../]

    [../]

    type = DirichletBC

    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]

    value = 0

  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]

    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'

  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'

  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]

  [../]

    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    variable = disp_x

  [../]
  [./react_y]

    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D/exp_cartesian_5_25_rho_0_sample_6/mechanical.i

[Functions]

    type = PiecewiseMultilinear

  [../]
  [./psic]

    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_5_25_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]

    [../]

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]

    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]

    type = GenericFunctionMaterial

    prop_values = 'psic'

    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]

    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'

  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]

    data_file = ../gold/Gc_exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    d = d

    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]

    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]

    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]

      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
